00003| mod state;

00005| use linera_sdk::{
00006|     abi::WithContractAbi,
00007|     views::{RootView, View},
00008|     Contract, ContractRuntime,
00009| };
00010| 
00011| use linera_name_system::{Message, Operation};
00012| use self::state::{LineraNameSystemState, DomainRecord};
00013| 
00014| /// One year in microseconds (365 days)
00015| const ONE_YEAR_MICROS: u64 = 365 * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1_000_000;
00016| 
00017| pub struct LineraNameSystemContract {
00018|     state: LineraNameSystemState,
00019|     runtime: ContractRuntime<Self>,
00020| }
00021| 
00022| linera_sdk::contract!(LineraNameSystemContract);
00023| 
00024| impl WithContractAbi for LineraNameSystemContract {
00025|     type Abi = linera_name_system::LineraNameSystemAbi;
00026| }
00027| 
00028| impl LineraNameSystemContract {
00029|     /// Get the registry chain ID - this is always the chain where the application was created
00030|     fn registry_chain_id(&mut self) -> linera_sdk::linera_base_types::ChainId {
00031|         self.runtime.application_creator_chain_id()
00032|     }
00033| 
00034|     /// Get current timestamp in microseconds
00035|     fn current_time(&mut self) -> u64 {
00036|         self.runtime.system_time().micros()
00037|     }
00038| 
00039|     /// Check if a domain is expired
00040|     fn is_expired(&mut self, record: &DomainRecord) -> bool {
00041|         self.current_time() > record.expiration
00042|     }
00043| }
00044| 
00045| impl Contract for LineraNameSystemContract {
00046|     type Message = Message;
00047|     type Parameters = ();
00048|     type InstantiationArgument = ();
00049|     type EventValue = ();
00050| 
00051|     async fn load(runtime: ContractRuntime<Self>) -> Self {
00052|         let state = LineraNameSystemState::load(runtime.root_view_storage_context())
00053|             .await
00054|             .expect("Failed to load state");
00055|         LineraNameSystemContract { state, runtime }
00056|     }
00057| 
00058|     async fn instantiate(&mut self, _argument: Self::InstantiationArgument) {
00059|         // Nothing to initialize - registry chain is derived from application_id
00060|     }
00061| 
00062|     async fn execute_operation(&mut self, operation: Self::Operation) -> Self::Response {
00063|         let owner = self.runtime.authenticated_signer()
00064|             .expect("Operation must be signed")
00065|             .to_string();
00066|         
00067|         let current_chain = self.runtime.chain_id();
00068|         let registry_chain_id = self.registry_chain_id();
00069| 
00070|         match operation {
00071|             Operation::Register { name } => {
00072|                 // Validate domain name
00073|                 assert!(!name.is_empty(), "Domain name cannot be empty");
00074|                 assert!(name.len() <= 63, "Domain name too long");
00075|                 assert!(
00076|                     name.chars().all(|c| c.is_ascii_alphanumeric() || c == '-'),
00077|                     "Invalid characters in domain name"
00078|                 );
00079| 
00080|                 if current_chain == registry_chain_id {
00081|                     // We ARE the registry chain - register directly
00082|                     let existing = self.state.domains.get(&name).await.expect("Failed to read state");
00083|                     
00084|                     // Check if domain exists and is not expired
00085|                     if let Some(record) = existing {
00086|                         if !self.is_expired(&record) {
00087|                             panic!("Domain already registered and not expired");
00088|                         }
00089|                     }
00090|                     
00091|                     // Register the domain with 1 year expiration
00092|                     let expiration = self.current_time() + ONE_YEAR_MICROS;
00093|                     let record = DomainRecord {
00094|                         owner,
00095|                         owner_chain_id: current_chain,
00096|                         expiration,
00097|                         price: 0,
00098|                         value: String::new(),
00099|                     };
00100|                     self.state.domains.insert(&name, record).expect("Failed to register domain");
00101|                 } else {
00102|                     // Send registration request to registry chain
00103|                     let message = Message::RequestRegister {
00104|                         name,
00105|                         owner,
00106|                         requester_chain: current_chain,
00107|                     };
00108|                     self.runtime.send_message(registry_chain_id, message);
00109|                 }
00110|             }
00111|             Operation::Transfer { name, new_owner } => {
00112|                 if current_chain == registry_chain_id {
00113|                     // We ARE the registry chain - transfer directly

00234|     async fn execute_message(&mut self, message: Self::Message) {
00235|         let current_chain = self.runtime.chain_id();
00236|         let registry_chain_id = self.registry_chain_id();
00237|         let current_time = self.current_time();
00238| 
00239|         match message {
00240|             Message::RequestRegister { name, owner, requester_chain } => {
00241|                 assert_eq!(current_chain, registry_chain_id, "Only registry chain can process registrations");
00242|                 
00243|                 let existing = self.state.domains.get(&name).await.expect("Failed to read state");
00244|                 
00245|                 // Check if domain exists and is not expired
00246|                 if let Some(record) = existing {
00247|                     if current_time <= record.expiration {
00248|                         let response = Message::RegistrationFailed {
00249|                             name,
00250|                             reason: "Domain already registered and not expired".to_string(),
00251|                         };
00252|                         self.runtime.send_message(requester_chain, response);
00253|                         return;
00254|                     }
00255|                 }
00256|                 
00257|                 // Register the domain with 1 year expiration
00258|                 let expiration = current_time + ONE_YEAR_MICROS;
00259|                 let record = DomainRecord {
00260|                     owner,
00261|                     owner_chain_id: requester_chain,
00262|                     expiration,
00263|                     price: 0,
00264|                     value: String::new(),
00265|                 };
00266|                 self.state.domains.insert(&name, record).expect("Failed to register domain");
00267|                 let response = Message::RegistrationSuccess { name };
00268|                 self.runtime.send_message(requester_chain, response);
00269|             }
00270|             Message::RequestTransfer { name, new_owner, current_owner, requester_chain } => {
00271|                 assert_eq!(current_chain, registry_chain_id, "Only registry chain can process transfers");
00272|                 
00273|                 let stored = self.state.domains.get(&name).await.expect("Failed to read state");
00274|                 match stored {
00275|                     None => {
00276|                         let response = Message::TransferFailed {
00277|                             name,
00278|                             reason: "Domain not registered".to_string(),
00279|                         };
00280|                         self.runtime.send_message(requester_chain, response);
00281|                     }
00282|                     Some(record) if current_time > record.expiration => {
00283|                         let response = Message::TransferFailed {
00284|                             name,
00285|                             reason: "Domain has expired".to_string(),
00286|                         };
00287|                         self.runtime.send_message(requester_chain, response);
00288|                     }
00289|                     Some(record) if record.owner != current_owner => {
00290|                         let response = Message::TransferFailed {
00291|                             name,
00292|                             reason: "Not the domain owner".to_string(),
00293|                         };
00294|                         self.runtime.send_message(requester_chain, response);
00295|                     }
00296|                     Some(mut record) => {
00297|                         record.owner = new_owner.clone();
00298|                         record.price = 0;
00299|                         self.state.domains.insert(&name, record).expect("Failed to transfer domain");
00300|                         let response = Message::TransferSuccess { name, new_owner };
00301|                         self.runtime.send_message(requester_chain, response);
00302|                     }
00303|                 }
00304|             }
00305|             Message::RequestExtend { name, owner, years, requester_chain } => {
00306|                 assert_eq!(current_chain, registry_chain_id, "Only registry chain can process extensions");

00219|       console.error("Failed to fetch all domains:", err);
00220|     } finally {
00221|       setIsLoadingDomains(false);
00222|     }
00223|   }, [appConnected, registryChainId, applicationId]);
00224| 
00225|   // Fetch balance when chain is connected
00226|   useEffect(() => {
00227|     if (chainConnected) {
00228|       fetchBalance();
00229|     }
00230|   }, [chainConnected, fetchBalance]);
00231| 
00232|   // Fetch registry info when app is connected
00233|   useEffect(() => {
00234|     if (appConnected) {
00235|       fetchRegistryInfo();
00236|     }
00237|   }, [appConnected, fetchRegistryInfo]);
00238| 
00239|   // Fetch all domains when registry chain ID is available
00240|   useEffect(() => {
00241|     if (appConnected && registryChainId) {
00242|       fetchAllDomains();
00243|     }
00244|   }, [appConnected, registryChainId, fetchAllDomains]);
00245| 
00246|   async function handleCheckDomain() {
00247|     if (!domainName.trim()) {
00248|       setError("Please enter a domain name");
00249|       return;
00250|     }
00251|     if (!registryChainId) {
00252|       setError("Registry chain ID not available yet");
00253|       return;
00254|     }
00255|     setIsSearching(true);
00256|     setError(null);
00257|     setSearchResult(null);
00258| 
00259|     try {
00260|       // Query the registry chain directly for authoritative data
00261|       const result = await lineraAdapter.queryApplicationOnChain<{
00262|         data?: { domain?: ExtendedDomainInfo; isAvailable: boolean };
00263|         errors?: Array<{ message: string }>;
00264|       }>(
00265|         registryChainId,
00266|         applicationId,
00267|         `query { domain(name: "${domainName.trim()}") { name owner ownerChainId expiration isExpired price isForSale value } isAvailable(name: "${domainName.trim()}") }`,
00268|       );
00269|       if (result.errors?.length) {
00270|         throw new Error(result.errors[0].message);
00271|       }
00272|       setSearchResult({
00273|         IsAvailable: result.data?.isAvailable,
00274|         domain: result.data?.domain,
00275|       });
00276|     } catch (err) {
00277|       console.error("Failed to check domain:", err);
00278|       setError(
00279|         err instanceof Error
00280|           ? err.message
00281|           : "Failed to check domain availability",
00282|       );
00283|     } finally {
00284|       setIsSearching(false);
00285|     }
00286|   }
00287| 
00288|   async function handleRegisterDomain() {
00289|     if (!domainName.trim()) {
00290|       setError("Please enter a domain name");
00291|       return;
00292|     }
00293|     if (!registryChainId) {
00294|       setError("Registry chain ID not available yet");
00295|       return;
00296|     }
00297|     setIsRegistering(true);
00298|     setError(null);
00299| 
00300|     try {
00301|       const result = await lineraAdapter.queryApplication<{
00302|         data?: { register: boolean };
00303|         errors?: Array<{ message: string }>;
00304|       }>({
00305|         query: `mutation { register(name: "${domainName.trim()}") }`,
00306|       });
00307| 
00308|       if (result.errors?.length) {
00309|         throw new Error(result.errors[0].message);
00310|       }
00311| 
00312|       if (result.data?.register) {
00313|         setSearchResult({ IsAvailable: false });
00314|         setError(null);
00315|         alert(
00316|           `Domain ${domainName.trim()}.linera registration submitted! Waiting for cross-chain sync...`,
00317|         );
00318| 
00319|         // Poll for the registration to appear on the registry chain
00320|         // Cross-chain messages may take several seconds to propagate
00321|         let attempts = 0;
00322|         const maxAttempts = 10;
00323|         const pollInterval = 3000; // 3 seconds between polls
00324| 
00325|         const pollRegistration = async (): Promise<boolean> => {
00326|           attempts++;
00327|           console.log(
00328|             `Polling for registration (attempt ${attempts}/${maxAttempts})...`,
00329|           );
00330| 
00331|           try {
00332|             const checkResult = await lineraAdapter.queryApplicationOnChain<{
00333|               data?: { isAvailable: boolean };
00334|               errors?: Array<{ message: string }>;
00335|             }>(
00336|               registryChainId,
00337|               applicationId,
00338|               `query { isAvailable(name: "${domainName.trim()}") }`,
00339|             );
00340| 
00341|             // If domain is no longer available, registration succeeded
00342|             if (checkResult.data?.isAvailable === false) {
00343|               console.log("Registration confirmed on registry chain!");
00344|               return true;
00345|             }
00346|           } catch (err) {
00347|             console.log("Poll attempt failed:", err);
00348|           }
00349| 
00350|           if (attempts < maxAttempts) {
00351|             await new Promise((resolve) => setTimeout(resolve, pollInterval));
00352|             return pollRegistration();
00353|           }
00354| 
00355|           return false;
00356|         };
00357| 
00358|         // Start polling after a short initial delay
00359|         setTimeout(async () => {
00360|           const confirmed = await pollRegistration();
00361|           if (confirmed) {
00362|             fetchAllDomains();
00363|           } else {
00364|             console.log(
00365|               "Registration not yet confirmed. Please refresh manually.",
00366|             );
00367|             fetchAllDomains(); // Try to fetch anyway
00368|           }
00369|         }, 2000);
00370|       }
00371|     } catch (err) {
00372|       console.error("Failed to register domain:", err);
00373|       setError(
00374|         err instanceof Error ? err.message : "Failed to register domain",
00375|       );
00376|     } finally {
00377|       setIsRegistering(false);
00378|     }
00379|   }
00380| 
00381|   async function handleLookupOwner() {
00382|     if (!domainName.trim()) {
00383|       setError("Please enter a domain name");
00384|       return;
00385|     }
00386|     if (!registryChainId) {
00387|       setError("Registry chain ID not available yet");
00388|       return;
00389|     }
00390|     setIsSearching(true);
00391|     setError(null);
00392|     setSearchResult(null);
00393| 
00394|     try {
00395|       // Query the registry chain directly for authoritative data
00396|       const result = await lineraAdapter.queryApplicationOnChain<{
00397|         data?: { domain?: ExtendedDomainInfo; owner: string | null };
00398|         errors?: Array<{ message: string }>;
00399|       }>(
00400|         registryChainId,
00401|         applicationId,
00402|         `query { domain(name: "${domainName.trim()}") { name owner ownerChainId expiration isExpired price isForSale value } owner(name: "${domainName.trim()}") }`,
00403|       );
00404|       if (result.errors?.length) {
00405|         throw new Error(result.errors[0].message);
00406|       }
00407|       setSearchResult({
00408|         Owner: result.data?.owner,
00409|         domain: result.data?.domain,
00410|       });
00411|     } catch (err) {
00412|       console.error("Failed to lookup owner:", err);
00413|       setError(
00414|         err instanceof Error ? err.message : "Failed to lookup domain owner",
00415|       );
00416|     } finally {
00417|       setIsSearching(false);
00418|     }
00419|   }
00420| 
00421|   async function handleExtendDomain(name: string) {
00422|     setIsExtending(true);
00423|     setError(null);
00424|     try {
00425|       const result = await lineraAdapter.queryApplication<{
00426|         data?: { extend: boolean };
00427|         errors?: Array<{ message: string }>;
00428|       }>({
00429|         query: `mutation { extend(name: "${name}", years: ${extendYears}) }`,
00430|       });
00431| 
00432|       if (result.errors?.length) {
00433|         throw new Error(result.errors[0].message);
00434|       }
00435| 
00436|       if (result.data?.extend) {
00437|         alert(`Domain ${name}.linera extended by ${extendYears} year(s)!`);
00438|         setTimeout(() => fetchAllDomains(), 2000);
00439|       }
00440|     } catch (err) {
00441|       console.error("Failed to extend domain:", err);
00442|       setError(err instanceof Error ? err.message : "Failed to extend domain");
00443|     } finally {
00444|       setIsExtending(false);
00445|       setShowDomainModal(false);
00446|     }
00447|   }
00448|

00451|     setError(null);
00452|     try {
00453|       const result = await lineraAdapter.queryApplication<{
00454|         data?: { setPrice: boolean };
00455|         errors?: Array<{ message: string }>;
00456|       }>({
00457|         query: `mutation { setPrice(name: "${name}", price: "${newPrice}") }`,
00458|       });
00459| 
00460|       if (result.errors?.length) {
00461|         throw new Error(result.errors[0].message);
00462|       }
00463| 
00464|       if (result.data?.setPrice) {
00465|         alert(`Domain ${name}.linera price set to ${newPrice}!`);
00466|         setTimeout(() => fetchAllDomains(), 2000);
00467|       }
00468|     } catch (err) {
00469|       console.error("Failed to set price:", err);
00470|       setError(err instanceof Error ? err.message : "Failed to set price");
00471|     } finally {
00472|       setIsSettingPrice(false);
00473|       setShowDomainModal(false);
00474|     }
00475|   }

00477|   async function handleBuyDomain(name: string) {
00478|     if (!confirm(`Are you sure you want to buy ${name}.linera?`)) {
00479|       return;
00480|     }
00481|     setIsBuying(true);
00482|     setError(null);
00483|     try {
00484|       const result = await lineraAdapter.queryApplication<{
00485|         data?: { buy: boolean };
00486|         errors?: Array<{ message: string }>;
00487|       }>({
00488|         query: `mutation { buy(name: "${name}") }`,
00489|       });
00490| 
00491|       if (result.errors?.length) {
00492|         throw new Error(result.errors[0].message);
00493|       }
00494| 
00495|       if (result.data?.buy) {
00496|         alert(`Domain ${name}.linera purchased successfully!`);
00497|         setTimeout(() => fetchAllDomains(), 2000);
00498|       }
00499|     } catch (err) {
00500|       console.error("Failed to buy domain:", err);
00501|       setError(err instanceof Error ? err.message : "Failed to buy domain");
00502|     } finally {
00503|       setIsBuying(false);
00504|       setShowDomainModal(false);
00505|     }
00506|   }
00507|

00536|   async function handleTransferDomain(name: string) {
00537|     if (!transferAddress.trim()) {
00538|       setError("Please enter a recipient address");
00539|       return;
00540|     }
00541|     if (
00542|       !confirm(
00543|         `Are you sure you want to transfer ${name}.linera to ${transferAddress}? This action cannot be undone.`,
00544|       )
00545|     ) {
00546|       return;
00547|     }
00548|     setIsTransferring(true);
00549|     setError(null);
00550|     try {
00551|       const result = await lineraAdapter.queryApplication<{
00552|         data?: { transfer: boolean };
00553|         errors?: Array<{ message: string }>;
00554|       }>({
00555|         query: `mutation { transfer(name: "${name}", newOwner: "${transferAddress.trim()}") }`,
00556|       });
00557| 
00558|       if (result.errors?.length) {
00559|         throw new Error(result.errors[0].message);
00560|       }
00561| 
00562|       if (result.data?.transfer) {
00563|         alert(
00564|           `Domain ${name}.linera transferred to ${transferAddress} successfully!`,
00565|         );
00566|         setTransferAddress("");
00567|         setTimeout(() => fetchAllDomains(), 2000);
00568|       }
00569|     } catch (err) {
00570|       console.error("Failed to transfer domain:", err);
00571|       setError(
00572|         err instanceof Error ? err.message : "Failed to transfer domain",
00573|       );
00574|     } finally {
00575|       setIsTransferring(false);
00576|       setShowDomainModal(false);
00577|     }
00578|   }
00579| 
00580|   function formatExpiration(timestamp: number): string {
00581|     const date = new Date(timestamp / 1000);
00582|     return date.toLocaleDateString();
00583|   }
00584| 
00585|   function openDomainModal(domain: ExtendedDomainInfo) {
00586|     setSelectedDomain(domain);
00587|     setNewPrice(domain.isForSale ? domain.price : "");
00588|     setNewValue(domain.value);
00589|     setShowDomainModal(true);
00590|   }
00591| 
00592|   return (
00593|     <div className="flex min-h-screen items-center justify-center bg-zinc-50 font-sans dark:bg-black">
00594|       <div className="w-full max-w-3xl px-6 py-12">
00595|         <div className="rounded-xl bg-white p-8 shadow-lg dark:bg-zinc-900">
00596|           <div className="mb-8 flex items-center justify-between">
00597|             <h1 className="text-3xl font-bold text-zinc-900 dark:text-white">
00598|               Linera Name System
00599|             </h1>
00600|             <DynamicWidget />
00601|           </div>
00602| 
00603|           <div className="mb-8">
00604|             <p className="mb-2 text-zinc-600 dark:text-zinc-400">
00605|               Register your unique .linera domain on the Linera blockchain.
00606|             </p>
00607|             <p className="text-zinc-600 dark:text-zinc-400">
00608|               Connect your wallet to get started. Your chain will be
00609|               automatically claimed from the testnet faucet.
00610|             </p>
00611|           </div>
00612| 
00613|           {error && (
00614|             <div className="mb-6 rounded-lg bg-red-50 p-4 dark:bg-red-900/20">
00615|               <p className="text-red-500 dark:text-red-300">{error}</p>
00616|             </div>
00617|           )}
00618| 
00619|           {/* Connection Status */}
00620|           {mounted && isAutoConnecting && (
00621|             <div className="mb-6 flex items-center justify-center gap-2 rounded-lg bg-sky-50 p-4 dark:bg-sky-900/20">
00622|               <div className="h-4 w-4 animate-spin rounded-full border-2 border-sky-600 border-t-transparent" />
00623|               <p className="text-sky-600 dark:text-sky-400">
00624|                 Connecting to Linera testnet...
00625|               </p>
00626|             </div>
00627|           )}
00628| 
00629|           {mounted && !isLoggedIn && (
00630|             <div className="mb-6 rounded-lg bg-zinc-100 p-6 text-center dark:bg-zinc-800">
00631|               <p className="text-zinc-500 dark:text-zinc-400">
00632|                 Please connect your wallet using the button above to get
00633|                 started.
00634|               </p>
00635|             </div>
00636|           )}
00637| 
00638|           {/* Domain Registration UI */}
00639|           {chainConnected && appConnected && (
00640|             <div className="space-y-6">
00641|               <div className="rounded-lg bg-zinc-100 p-6 dark:bg-zinc-800">
00642|                 <h2 className="mb-4 text-lg font-semibold text-zinc-900 dark:text-white">
00643|                   Search & Register Domain
00644|                 </h2>
00645|                 <div className="flex gap-2">
00646|                   <div className="relative flex-1">
00647|                     <input
00648|                       type="text"
00649|                       value={domainName}
00650|                       onChange={(e) =>
00651|                         setDomainName(
00652|                           e.target.value
00653|                             .toLowerCase()
00654|                             .replace(/[^a-z0-9-]/g, ""),
00655|                         )
00656|                       }
00657|                       placeholder="Enter domain name"
00658|                       className="w-full rounded-lg border border-zinc-300 bg-white px-4 py-3 pr-20 text-zinc-900 placeholder-zinc-400 focus:border-sky-500 focus:outline-none focus:ring-1 focus:ring-sky-500 dark:border-zinc-600 dark:bg-zinc-900 dark:text-white dark:placeholder-zinc-500"
00659|                     />
00660|                     <span className="absolute right-4 top-1/2 -translate-y-1/2 text-zinc-400 dark:text-zinc-500">
00661|                       .linera
00662|                     </span>
00663|                   </div>
00664|                 </div>
00665|                 <div className="mt-4 flex gap-2">
00666|                   <button
00667|                     type="button"
00668|                     onClick={handleCheckDomain}
00669|                     disabled={isSearching || !domainName.trim()}
00670|                     className="flex-1 rounded-lg bg-zinc-200 px-4 py-2 font-medium text-zinc-800 transition-colors hover:bg-zinc-300 disabled:cursor-not-allowed disabled:opacity-50 dark:bg-zinc-700 dark:text-zinc-200 dark:hover:bg-zinc-600"
00671|                   >
00672|                     {isSearching ? "Checking..." : "Check Availability"}
00673|                   </button>
00674|                   <button
00675|                     type="button"
00676|                     onClick={handleLookupOwner}
00677|                     disabled={isSearching || !domainName.trim()}
00678|                     className="flex-1 rounded-lg bg-zinc-200 px-4 py-2 font-medium text-zinc-800 transition-colors hover:bg-zinc-300 disabled:cursor-not-allowed disabled:opacity-50 dark:bg-zinc-700 dark:text-zinc-200 dark:hover:bg-zinc-600"
00679|                   >
00680|                     Lookup Owner
00681|                   </button>
00682|                 </div>
00683| 
00684|                 {searchResult && (
00685|                   <div className="mt-4 rounded-lg bg-white p-4 dark:bg-zinc-900">
00686|                     {searchResult.IsAvailable !== undefined &&
00687|                       searchResult.IsAvailable && (
00688|                         <div className="flex items-center justify-between">
00689|                           <div>
00690|                             <p className="font-medium text-zinc-900 dark:text-white">
00691|                               {domainName}.linera
00692|                             </p>
00693|                             <p className="text-green-600 dark:text-green-400">
00694|                               Available!
00695|                             </p>
00696|                           </div>
00697|                           <button
00698|                             type="button"
00699|                             onClick={handleRegisterDomain}
00700|                             disabled={isRegistering}
00701|                             className="rounded-lg bg-sky-600 px-6 py-2 font-medium text-white transition-colors hover:bg-sky-700 disabled:cursor-not-allowed disabled:opacity-50"
00702|                           >
00703|                             {isRegistering ? "Registering..." : "Register"}
00704|                           </button>
00705|                         </div>
00706|                       )}
00707|                     {searchResult.domain && (
00708|                       <div>
00709|                         <p className="font-medium text-zinc-900 dark:text-white">
00710|                           {searchResult.domain.name}.linera
00711|                         </p>
00712|                         <p className="text-sm text-zinc-500 dark:text-zinc-400">
00713|                           Owner:
00714|                         </p>
00715|                         <p className="break-all font-mono text-sm text-zinc-700 dark:text-zinc-300 mb-2">
00716|                           {searchResult.domain.owner}
00717|                         </p>
00718|                         <div className="space-y-1 text-xs text-zinc-600 dark:text-zinc-400">
00719|                           <p>
00720|                             Expires:{" "}
00721|                             {formatExpiration(searchResult.domain.expiration)}
00722|                           </p>
00723|                           <p
00724|                             className={
00725|                               searchResult.domain.isExpired
00726|                                 ? "text-red-500 dark:text-red-400"
00727|                                 : ""
00728|                             }
00729|                           >
00730|                             Status:{" "}
00731|                             {searchResult.domain.isExpired
00732|                               ? "Expired"
00733|                               : "Active"}
00734|                           </p>
00735|                           <p>
00736|                             {searchResult.domain.isForSale
00737|                               ? `Price: ${searchResult.domain.price} LINERA`
00738|                               : "Not for sale"}
00739|                           </p>
00740|                           <p>
00741|                             Value: {searchResult.domain.value || "(not set)"}
00742|                           </p>
00743|                         </div>
00744|                       </div>
00745|                     )}
00746|                   </div>
00747|                 )}
00748|               </div>
00749| 
00750|               {/* All Registered Domains */}
00751|               <div className="rounded-lg bg-zinc-100 p-6 dark:bg-zinc-800">
00752|                 <div className="mb-4 flex items-center justify-between">
00753|                   <h2 className="text-lg font-semibold text-zinc-900 dark:text-white">
00754|                     Registered Domains
00755|                   </h2>
00756|                   <button
00757|                     type="button"
00758|                     onClick={fetchAllDomains}
00759|                     disabled={isLoadingDomains}
00760|                     className="rounded-lg bg-zinc-200 px-3 py-1 text-sm font-medium text-zinc-700 transition-colors hover:bg-zinc-300 disabled:opacity-50 dark:bg-zinc-700 dark:text-zinc-300 dark:hover:bg-zinc-600"
00761|                   >
00762|                     {isLoadingDomains ? "Loading..." : "Refresh"}
00763|                   </button>
00764|                 </div>
00765|                 {allDomains.length === 0 ? (
00766|                   <p className="text-zinc-500 dark:text-zinc-400">
00767|                     {isLoadingDomains
00768|                       ? "Loading domains..."
00769|                       : "No domains registered yet."}
00770|                   </p>
00771|                 ) : (
00772|                   <ul className="max-h-64 space-y-2 overflow-y-auto">
00773|                     {allDomains.map((domain) => (
00774|                       <li
00775|                         key={domain.name}
00776|                         onClick={() => openDomainModal(domain)}
00777|                         onKeyDown={(e) =>
00778|                           e.key === "Enter" && openDomainModal(domain)
00779|                         }
00780|                         className="cursor-pointer rounded-lg bg-white p-3 dark:bg-zinc-900 hover:bg-zinc-50 dark:hover:bg-zinc-800 transition-colors"
00781|                       >
00782|                         <div className="flex items-center justify-between">
00783|                           <div>
00784|                             <p className="font-medium text-zinc-900 dark:text-white">
00785|                               {domain.name}.linera
00786|                             </p>
00787|                             <p className="truncate text-xs text-zinc-500 dark:text-zinc-400">
00788|                               Owner: {domain.owner.slice(0, 16)}...
00789|                               {domain.owner.slice(-8)}
00790|                             </p>
00791|                           </div>
00792|                           <div className="text-right text-xs">
00793|                             <p
00794|                               className={
00795|                                 domain.isExpired
00796|                                   ? "text-red-500 dark:text-red-400"
00797|                                   : "text-green-500 dark:text-green-400"
00798|                               }
00799|                             >
00800|                               {domain.isExpired ? "Expired" : "Active"}
00801|                             </p>
00802|                             {domain.isForSale && (
00803|                               <p className="text-sky-600 dark:text-sky-400">
00804|                                 {domain.price} LINERA
00805|                               </p>
00806|                             )}
00807|                           </div>
00808|                         </div>
00809|                       </li>
00810|                     ))}
00811|                   </ul>
00812|                 )}
00813|               </div>
00814|             </div>
00815|           )}
00816| 
00817|           {/* Domain Management Modal */}

## Assistant

Looking at the context, I can see that the "Set Price" operation showed an alert saying "Domain panda.linera price set to 0.01!" but when checking the domain data, the price is still "0" and `isForSale` is `false`. This indicates the price was not actually updated on the registry chain.

Let me check the service.rs to see how the `setPrice` mutation is implemented:

**Tool Call: contracts/linera_name_system/src/service.rs**
Status: Completed

00055|         let state = ctx.data_unchecked::<Arc<LineraNameSystemState>>();
00056|         state.domains.get(&name).await.ok().flatten().map(|r| r.owner)

00061|         let state = ctx.data_unchecked::<Arc<LineraNameSystemState>>();
00062|         let runtime = ctx.data_unchecked::<Arc<ServiceRuntime<LineraNameSystemService>>>();
00063|         let current_time = runtime.system_time().micros();
00064|         
00065|         match state.domains.get(&name).await.ok().flatten() {
00066|             None => true,
00067|             Some(record) => current_time > record.expiration,
00068|         }
00069|     }

00093|         let current_time = runtime.system_time().micros();

## Assistant

Looking at the code, I can see the issue. The `setPrice` mutation in `service.rs:234-239` parses the price as a string and converts it to `u128`. The frontend sends `"0.01"` as the price, but `"0.01".parse::<u128>()` will fail (since u128 doesn't support decimals) and default to `0`.

Let me create a todo list and fix this issue:

**Tool Call: 2 todos**

## Assistant

The issue is clear: the price is stored as `u128` (integer), but the frontend is sending decimal values like `"0.01"`. When parsing `"0.01"` as `u128`, it fails and defaults to `0`.

There are two approaches to fix this:
1. **Frontend fix**: Convert the decimal to the smallest unit (like wei in Ethereum) before sending
2. **Contract fix**: Parse the decimal string and convert to the smallest unit

The best approach is to handle this in the frontend by converting to the smallest unit. Let me check what unit LINERA uses and update the frontend to send the price in the smallest unit.

Looking at the code, the price is stored as `u128` which should represent the smallest unit. The frontend should multiply decimal values by the appropriate factor (e.g., 10^18 for most blockchains).

Let me fix the frontend to properly convert decimal prices:

**Tool Call: src/components/counter-app.tsx**
Status: Completed

```
  async function handleSetPrice(name: string) {
    setIsSettingPrice(true);
    setError(null);
    try {
      // Convert decimal price to smallest unit (18 decimals like most blockchains)
      // e.g., 0.01 LINERA = 10000000000000000 (0.01 * 10^18)
      const priceFloat = parseFloat(newPrice) || 0;
      const priceInSmallestUnit = BigInt(Math.floor(priceFloat * 1e18)).toString();
      
      const result = await lineraAdapter.queryApplication<{
        data?: { setPrice: boolean };
        errors?: Array<{ message: string }>;
      }>({
        query: `mutation { setPrice(name: "${name}", price: "${priceInSmallestUnit}") }`,
      });
```

Diff: /home/[USERNAME]/CascadeProjects/linera-name-system-worktree/src/components/counter-app.tsx
```
  function formatExpiration(timestamp: number): string {
    const date = new Date(timestamp / 1000);
    return date.toLocaleDateString();
  }

  // Convert price from smallest unit (u128) to human-readable format
  function formatPrice(priceStr: string): string {
    try {
      const price = BigInt(priceStr);
      if (price === 0n) return "0";
      // Convert from smallest unit (18 decimals) to human-readable
      const divisor = BigInt(1e18);
      const wholePart = price / divisor;
      const fractionalPart = price % divisor;
      if (fractionalPart === 0n) {
        return wholePart.toString();
      }
      // Format fractional part with up to 6 decimal places
      const fractionalStr = fractionalPart.toString().padStart(18, "0");
      const trimmed = fractionalStr.slice(0, 6).replace(/0+$/, "");
      if (trimmed === "") {
        return wholePart.toString();
      }
      return `${wholePart}.${trimmed}`;
    } catch {
      return priceStr;
    }
  }

  function openDomainModal(domain: ExtendedDomainInfo) {
    setSelectedDomain(domain);
    // Convert stored price to human-readable for the input field
    setNewPrice(domain.isForSale ? formatPrice(domain.price) : "");
    setNewValue(domain.value);
    setShowDomainModal(true);
  }
```


## Assistant

**Tool Call: src/components/counter-app.tsx**
Status: Completed



Diff: /home/[USERNAME]/CascadeProjects/linera-name-system-worktree/src/components/counter-app.tsx
```
  function formatExpiration(timestamp: number): string {
    const date = new Date(timestamp / 1000);
    return date.toLocaleDateString();
  }

  // Convert price from smallest unit (u128) to human-readable format
  function formatPrice(priceStr: string): string {
    try {
      const price = BigInt(priceStr);
      if (price === BigInt(0)) return "0";
      // Convert from smallest unit (18 decimals) to human-readable
      const divisor = BigInt("1000000000000000000"); // 10^18
      const wholePart = price / divisor;
      const fractionalPart = price % divisor;
      if (fractionalPart === BigInt(0)) {
        return wholePart.toString();
      }
      // Format fractional part with up to 6 decimal places
      const fractionalStr = fractionalPart.toString().padStart(18, "0");
      const trimmed = fractionalStr.slice(0, 6).replace(/0+$/, "");
      if (trimmed === "") {
        return wholePart.toString();
      }
      return `${wholePart}.${trimmed}`;
    } catch {
      return priceStr;
    }
  }

  function openDomainModal(domain: ExtendedDomainInfo) {
    setSelectedDomain(domain);
    // Convert stored price to human-readable for the input field
    setNewPrice(domain.isForSale ? formatPrice(domain.price) : "");
    setNewValue(domain.value);
    setShowDomainModal(true);
  }
```

## Assistant

Looking at the contract code, I can see the issue. The `record.owner` comparison at line 357 (`record.owner != owner`) is comparing the stored owner with the authenticated signer. The problem is likely a **case sensitivity issue** - the owner address stored in the domain might have different casing than what `authenticated_signer().to_string()` returns.

Let me check the console logs to see what's happening:
